       int key = v[left];\n        int i = left;\n        int j = right;\n        while (i < j) {\n            while (key <= v[j] && i < j) j--;\n            while (key >= v[i] && i < j)i++;\n            cout << i << \" \" << j << endl;\n            swap(v[i], v[j]);\n        }\n        swap(v[i], v[left]);\n        if (i == k) return v[i];\n        if (k < i) return quickSortGetK(v, left, i - 1, k);\n        else return  quickSortGetK(v, i + 1, right,k);\n    }\n    int main() {\n        vector<int> v;\n        for (int i = 0; i < 10; i++) {\n            int data;\n            cin >> data;\n sumå¼€çª—å¦‚ä½•å†™ï¼Ÿ\n\nåœ¨HiveSQLä¸­ï¼Œå¯ä»¥ä½¿ç”¨çª—å£å‡½æ•°æ¥è¿›è¡Œsumæ“ä½œã€‚ä¸‹é¢æ˜¯ä¸€ä¸ªç¤ºä¾‹ï¼š\n\n    \n    \n    SELECT column1, column2, SUM(column3) OVER (PARTITION BY column1 ORDER BY
